Overview\\n\\nThe Envoy access log formatting system is implemented across multiple source files in the `source/common/formatter/` directory. The system uses a two-level command parsing approach:\\n\\n1. **HTTP-specific commands** registered in `HttpBuiltInCommandParser` (source/common/formatter/http_specific_formatter.cc)\\n2. **Stream info commands** registered in `getKnownStreamInfoFormatterProviders()` (source/common/formatter/stream_info_formatter.cc)\\n\\n## Command Operator Implementation\\n\\n### HTTP-Specific Operators (%REQ%, %RESP%, etc.)\\n\\nThese are implemented in `source/common/formatter/http_specific_formatter.cc` via the `HttpBuiltInCommandParser::getKnownFormatters()` function, which registers the following command operators:\\n\\n- **%REQ(header-name)%** - Implemented via `RequestHeaderFormatter` class. Formats request headers with optional max length truncation.\\n- **%RESP(header-name)%** - Implemented via `ResponseHeaderFormatter` class. Formats response headers.\\n- **%TRAILER(header-name)%** - Implemented via `ResponseTrailerFormatter` class. Formats response trailers.\\n- **%LOCAL_REPLY_BODY%** - Implemented via `LocalReplyBodyFormatter` class.\\n- **%ACCESS_LOG_TYPE%** - Implemented via `AccessLogTypeFormatter` class.\\n- **%GRPC_STATUS%** - Implemented via `GrpcStatusFormatter` class. Supports CAMEL_STRING, SNAKE_STRING, and NUMBER formats.\\n- **%GRPC_STATUS_NUMBER%** - Shorthand for GRPC_STATUS with NUMBER format.\\n- **%REQUEST_HEADERS_BYTES%** - Implemented via `HeadersByteSizeFormatter`.\\n- **%RESPONSE_HEADERS_BYTES%** - Implemented via `HeadersByteSizeFormatter`.\\n- **%RESPONSE_TRAILERS_BYTES%** - Implemented via `HeadersByteSizeFormatter`.\\n- **%STREAM_INFO_REQ(header-name)%** - Alternative request header formatter using stream info.\\n- **%TRACE_ID%** - Implemented via `TraceIDFormatter` class.\\n\\n### Stream Info Operators (%DURATION%, %UPSTREAM_HOST%, etc.)\\n\\nThese are implemented in `source/common/formatter/stream_info_formatter.cc` via the `getKnownStreamInfoFormatterProviders()` function, which returns a `StreamInfoFormatterProviderLookupTable` (flat_hash_map) containing:\\n\\n#### Duration-Related Operators:\\n- **%REQUEST_DURATION%** - Time from first downstream RX byte to last downstream RX byte\\n- **%REQUEST_TX_DURATION%** - Time from first to last upstream TX byte\\n- **%RESPONSE_DURATION%** - Time from first upstream RX byte\\n- **%RESPONSE_TX_DURATION%** - Duration between downstream and upstream response\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_HANDSHAKE_DURATION%** - Downstream connection handshake duration\\n- **%ROUNDTRIP_DURATION%** - Complete roundtrip duration\\n- **%DURATION%** - Current request duration from stream info (line 1034-1041)\\n- **%COMMON_DURATION(...)%** - Configurable duration between arbitrary time points (line 1042-1046)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_CONNECTION_POOL_READY_DURATION%** - Connection pool callback latency (line 1737-1756)\\n\\n#### Bytes-Related Operators:\\n- **%BYTES_RECEIVED%** - Downstream bytes received\\n- **%BYTES_SENT%** - Downstream bytes sent\\n- **%BYTES_RETRANSMITTED%** - TCP retransmitted bytes\\n- **%PACKETS_RETRANSMITTED%** - TCP retransmitted packets\\n- **%UPSTREAM_WIRE_BYTES_RECEIVED%** - Upstream wire bytes received\\n- **%UPSTREAM_HEADER_BYTES_RECEIVED%** - Upstream header bytes received\\n- **%UPSTREAM_WIRE_BYTES_SENT%** - Upstream wire bytes sent\\n- **%UPSTREAM_HEADER_BYTES_SENT%** - Upstream header bytes sent\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_WIRE_BYTES_RECEIVED%** - Downstream wire bytes received\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_HEADER_BYTES_RECEIVED%** - Downstream header bytes received\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_WIRE_BYTES_SENT%** - Downstream wire bytes sent\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_HEADER_BYTES_SENT%** - Downstream header bytes sent\\n\\n#### Upstream Host and Connection Operators:\\n- **%UPSTREAM_HOST%** - Upstream host address with port (line 1084-1100, uses `StreamInfoAddressFormatterProvider`)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_HOST_NAME%** - Upstream host hostname or address (line 1063-1083)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_CLUSTER%** - Upstream cluster observability name (line 1114-1130)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_CLUSTER_RAW%** - Upstream cluster raw name (line 1131-1146)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_LOCAL_ADDRESS%** - Upstream local address with port (line 1147-1158)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_LOCAL_ADDRESS_WITHOUT_PORT%** - Upstream local address without port (line 1159-1170)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_LOCAL_PORT%** - Upstream local port only (line 1171-1182)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_REMOTE_ADDRESS%** - Upstream remote address with port (line 1183-1191)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_REMOTE_ADDRESS_WITHOUT_PORT%** - Upstream remote address without port (line 1192-1200)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_REMOTE_PORT%** - Upstream remote port only (line 1201-1209)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_CONNECTION_ID%** - Upstream connection ID (line 1101-1113)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_REQUEST_ATTEMPT_COUNT%** - Number of upstream request attempts (line 1210-1217)\\n\\n#### Protocol and Response Code Operators:\\n- **%PROTOCOL%** - Request protocol (HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, etc.)\\n- **%UPSTREAM_PROTOCOL%** - Upstream protocol\\n- **%RESPONSE_CODE%** - HTTP response status code\\n- **%RESPONSE_CODE_DETAILS%** - Response code details string\\n- **%CONNECTION_TERMINATION_DETAILS%** - Connection termination details\\n- **%RESPONSE_FLAGS%** - Response flags in short format\\n- **%RESPONSE_FLAGS_LONG%** - Response flags in long format\\n\\n#### Address Operators (Downstream):\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_LOCAL_ADDRESS%** - Downstream local address with port\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_LOCAL_ADDRESS_WITHOUT_PORT%** - Downstream local address without port\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_LOCAL_PORT%** - Downstream TLS cipher suite\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_TLS_VERSION%** - Downstream TLS version\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_TLS_SESSION_ID%** - Downstream TLS session ID\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_PEER_ISSUER%** - Downstream peer certificate issuer\\n- **%DOWNSTREAM_PEER_CERT%** -
